                      <div data-reactid="427">
                       Bright room on top floor of contemporary house. Next to large living room &amp;half bath. Two full bathrooms on lower floor. The best wifi and ethernet connections in the house with the main modem on your desk. To see more rooms, click on host photo.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="428">
                       Our home is on one acre on a hill overlooking the hills of Dodger Stadium and downtown L.A. in the background. From the back of the house, you have views of our own hill and canyon. It's possible to hike up to the top and also across the open hill for more views. You can see to Long Beach and Catalina Island on clear days from our kitchen windows. The house is large, spacious, and uncluttered. The neighborhood is very quiet and peaceful.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="429">
                       It's an interesting place for walks, with beautiful views. There is a nearby natural hiking park within a four minute walk, Elyria Canyon Park. We have a nice public library beside the bus stop near our house. There are also shops and restaurants within a ten minute walk. It feels like we are out in the country from the views and nature around us, even though we are right in L.A. and close to everything L.A. has to offer.

                       Our Mount Washington home is on one acre, on a hill overlooking the hills of Dodger Stadium across the valley and downtown L.A. in the background.                      <div data-reactid="1934">
                      <div data-reactid="1935">
                       Fully appointed loft with 22' ceilings and huge windows. A private bedroom along side stainless kitchen, rustic dining and eclectic living space. Located near public transportation and plenty of parking. Please see our private room listing.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1936">
                       So much to see just steps outside the front door. Public yet private garden spaces, a fun restaurant bar, climbing gym, outdoor art installations and a direct bus line to Union Station. All within a two minute walk.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1937">
                       Located in one of the oldest neighborhoods in LA, there is amazing history to be seen near-by. Public parks are a bike ride away. You can find yourself in the heart of downtown in minutes. Local eateries are close or ask the host for the personal chef experience.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1938">
                       <li data-reactid="1939"><p data-reactid="1940">Quint met us out front, made us feel welcome and gave us initial instructions. Let me start with what we liked: i) the loft is a lot of space for the money with a large well equipped kitchen, sunken living room, dining area and bathroom. There is also a good sized bedroom with a reasonably comfortable bed -- though no window to the outside. ii) Kitchen is unusually well equipped and would be very good for anyone who wanted to cook. iv) Unit is located in a former brewary that has been converted to a very large artist's colony with many separate studios, iv) Barbara's Brewery &amp; restaurant is only about 200 feet from the unit's front door and they have terrific, reasonably priced food and beer. On the down side: i) unit is quite dark with not much natural or electric light, ii) unit is not really completely private since the loft space is entered through an open staircase from the lower floor. Quint and/or his companion were frequency working there (though they were quiet), iii) housekeeping left a little to be desired, iv) approach to the unit through the artist's colony is a little complex though interesting. If you just want a simple place to rest your weary head you probably should look elsewhere.</p><span data-reactid="1941">Michael</span><span data-reactid="1942">2016-04-06T00:00:00Z</span></li>

I will absolutely be back and looking forward to it! **Just a heads up for some-- it's not an entire apartment but a shared space and you get 1 bedroom!!</p><span data-reactid="1949">Ting</span><span data-reactid="1950">2017-03-19T00:00:00Z</span></li>
